			function EndRequestHandler(sender, args) {
				var error = args.get_error();
				if (error) {
					args.set_errorHandled(true);
					var message = '';
					for (var errorMember in error) {
						message += '\t' + errorMember + ':' + error[errorMember] + '\n';
					}

					ErrorManager(GetCurrentUrl() + "/WebServicesPublic.asmx/LogJavaScriptError")
						.SendError(message, "", "");
				}
			}

			function InitializeErrorManager() {
				ErrorManager(GetCurrentUrl() + "/WebServicesPublic.asmx/LogJavaScriptError").Initialize();
			}
			
			function GetCurrentUrl() {
				return $(location).prop("protocol") + "//" + $(location).prop("host");
			}

			InitializeErrorManager();

			<h1 class="title">
				<span id="plcContent_lblPageTitle">Nursing Plan of Care Recorder</span>

	<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" class="content-table">
		<tbody><tr>
			<td class="menu-cell">
				<div class="menu-panel">
					
					

					<div id="plcContent_plcContent_ctlAlternateMenu_pnlAlternateMenu">
	
		
			
		
		
		<div class="alternate-menu" id="plcContent_plcContent_ctlAlternateMenu_ctlMenuGroupAcceliTrackScheduler_pnlAlternateMenuGroup">
		<div style="display:block;" class="alternate-menu-group" id="plcContent_plcContent_ctlAlternateMenu_ctlMenuGroupAcceliTrackScheduler_pnlAlternateMenuGroup_pnlContent">
			
		
				<div class="alternate-menu-item">
					<a href="../Calendar.aspx?DragAndDrop=true" id="plcContent_plcContent_ctlAlternateMenu_ctlMenuGroupAcceliTrackScheduler_pnlAlternateMenuGroup_rptAlternateMenu_lnkAlternateMenu_0">Drag &amp; Drop Scheduler</a>

<script type="text/javascript">
	/* This method is identical to the method in the MS javascript lib except that it adds a click function to anchors in non-IE browsers */
	var __defaultFired = false;
	function WebForm_FireDefaultButton(event, target) {
		var element = event.target || event.srcElement;
		if (!__defaultFired &amp;&amp; event.keyCode == 13 &amp;&amp; !(element &amp;&amp; (element.tagName.toLowerCase() == "textarea"))) {
			var defaultButton;
			if (__nonMSDOMBrowser) {
				defaultButton = document.getElementById(target);
			} else {
				defaultButton = document.all[target];
			}

			/* This is the only addition to this method, the rest is identical to MS version.*/
			if (defaultButton &amp;&amp; typeof (defaultButton.click) == "undefined") {
				defaultButton.click = function() {
					var result = true;
					if (defaultButton.onclick)
						result = b.onclick();
					if (typeof (result) == "undefined" || result)
						eval(unescape(defaultButton.href.substr(11)));
				};
			}

			if (defaultButton &amp;&amp; typeof (defaultButton.click) != "undefined") {
				defaultButton.click();
				event.cancelBubble = true;
				if (event.stopPropagation) event.stopPropagation();
				return false;
			}
		}
		return true;
	}
</script>
